***драматический.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:драматический.html>драмати́ческий</a> (9802)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">dramat(ique)</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драматический.html>драмати́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dramatíčeskij</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>драп</a> (32051)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1787. Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>drap</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>драп</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>drap</a></span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>дра́па</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>дра́пы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>дра́пов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>thick woolen cloth</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дра́повый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">drápovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драпать.html>дра́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drápatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to skedaddle, to hightail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*drapati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>драп</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>drap</a></span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>дра́па</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>дра́пы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>дра́пов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fleeing, skedaddling, runner <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">as in “to do a runner”</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>дра́пу</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">datʹ <b>drápu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>flee</b>, to make a <b>run for it</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Romani_language" class="extiw" title="w:Romani language">Romani</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="rom">drab</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">medicine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, attested no later than 1981.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>драп</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>drap</a></span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>дра́па</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>дра́пы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>дра́пов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> marijuana</li></ol>

***драпать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:драпать.html>дра́пать</a> (20496)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Presumably, with the original sense being “to tear, to scratch”, ultimately descends from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*drapati</i>; compare to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">drápat</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">drapać</i>; compare to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a> дёру</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ djóru</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удирать.html>удира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">udirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвануть.html>рвану́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rvanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:коготь.html>ко́гти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rvatʹ kógti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for other examples of mutation of “to tear” into “to flee”.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драпать.html>дра́пать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drápatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драпануть.html>драпану́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to skedaddle, to hightail, to flee</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>драп</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:драп.html>drap</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***драть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a> (9473)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">дра́ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dráti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dьràti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to tear, to flay</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dratʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to tear, to tear up, to tear to pieces
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:горло.html>го́рло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dratʹ</b> górlo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1)to bawl; scream one's lungs out; 2) shout songs</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разодрать.html>разодра́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razodrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to strip off, to tear off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лыко.html>лы́ко</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dratʹ</b> lýko</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bark lime trees</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шкура.html>шку́ру</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:овца.html>овцы́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dratʹ</b> škúru s ovcý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to flay a sheep</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шкура.html>шку́ру</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шкура.html>шку́ры</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:семь.html>семь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шкура.html>шку́р</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dratʹ</b> škúru (tri škúry, semʹ škur) s kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to skin someone alive</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:живой.html>живо́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мертвый.html>мёртвого</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dratʹ</b> s živóvo i mjórtvovo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fleece unmercifully</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отодрать.html>отодра́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otodrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ободрать.html>ободра́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obodrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pull out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зу́бы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dratʹ</b> zúby</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pull out teeth</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выдрать.html>вы́драть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výdratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to charge, to fleece, to rip off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:баснословный.html>басносло́вные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:процент.html>проце́нты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dratʹ</b> basnoslóvnyje procénty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to charge an incredible interest</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:содрать.html>содра́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sodrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(of wild animals)</i> to kill
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задрать.html>задра́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zadrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cause a stinging/burning pain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>дерёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:горло.html>го́рло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u menjá <b>derjót</b> górlo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I have a sore throat</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run away, to escape, to take flight
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лопатка.html>лопа́тки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dratʹ</b> vo vse lopátki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run as fast as one's legs can carry one</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удрать.html>удра́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">udrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to flog, to thrash, to give a flogging
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ши</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dratʹ</b> kovó-libo za úši (za vólosy)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pull someone's ears (hair)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">чёрт <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>дери́</a></b>!; чёрт <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>дра́л</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čórt jevó <b>derí</b>!; čórt by jevó <b>dral</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">damn/blast him!</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выдрать.html>вы́драть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výdratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:драться.html>дра́ться</a> (2368)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драться.html>дра́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подраться.html>подра́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fight, to scuffle</li>
<li>to struggle</li>
<li>to tear <i>(intransitive)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***драчун.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:драчун.html>драчу́н</a> (25225)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">драч-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drač-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́н</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ún</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare dialectal <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дра́ча</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dráča</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fight, scuffle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>fighter, brawler</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дребезг.html>дре́безг</a> (28856)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*drebězgъ</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дребезжать.html>дребезжа́ть</a> (8980)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Formed from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дребезг.html>дре́безг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drébezg</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jingle, tinkle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span>, <span class="ann-pos">stative suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The root is from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*drebězgъ</i>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">drebė̃znos</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">drebė̃nos</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">remnants</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*dreb-</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰrebʰ-</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>

</p>
<ol><li>to jingle, to tinkle</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:древесина.html>древеси́на</a> (14222)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древесина.html>древеси́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drevesína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древесина.html>древеси́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древесина.html>древеси́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древесина.html>древеси́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wood, wood material, wood substance</li>
<li>lignin</li>
<li>wood pulp, wood cellulose</li></ol>

<li><a class="mw-selflink selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:древесина.html>древеси́на</a></a> [1], <a href = vnd.unilang:выделенный.html>вы́деленная</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:отделённый.html>отделённая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:растение.html>расте́ния</a>} <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Не ожидаем мы и сокращения поставок <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">древесины</span>, продукции химической промышленности. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li>какой-либо материал строительного или хозяйственного назначения из древесины [1], либо совокупность таких материалов <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Заготавливать <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">древесину</span>. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:строительный.html>строи́тельное</a>">строит.</span> материал из древесины [1], в состав которого древесина [1] входит не в переработанном (измельчённом и склеенном) виде, а в исходном виде <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Материалом для шаблона может служить плотная <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">древесина</span> или лист ДСП (древесно-стружечной плиты). </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>

***древесный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сный</a> (10369)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drevésnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wood; woody, ligneous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:замазка.html>зама́зка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevésnaja</b> zamázka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wood cement, joiner’s putty</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сная</a></b> каме́дь</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevésnaja</b> kamédʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wood gum, xylan</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:масло.html>ма́сло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevésnoje</b> máslo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wood oil, tung oil</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:масса.html>ма́сса</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevésnaja</b> mássa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wood pulp</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мука.html>мука́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevésnaja</b> muká</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sawdust, wood meal</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:опилка.html>опи́лки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevésnyje</b> opílki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sawdust</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сахар.html>са́хар</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevésnyj</b> sáxar</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wood sugar, xylose</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спирт.html>спи́рт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevésnyj</b> spírt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wood alcohol, methyl alcohol</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стружка.html>стру́жка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevésnaja</b> strúžka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wood shavings, excelsior</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:топливо.html>то́пливо</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevésnoje</b> tóplivo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">firewood</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:уголь.html>у́голь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevésnyj</b> úgolʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">charcoal</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:уксус.html>у́ксус</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevésnyj</b> úksus</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wood vinegar, pyroligneous acid</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шерсть.html>ше́рсть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevésnaja</b> šérstʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">wood fiber, excelsior</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fibrous</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tree; arboreal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лягушка.html>лягу́шка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevésnaja</b> ljagúška</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tree frog</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:насаждение.html>насажде́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevésnoje</b> nasaždénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tree plantation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древесный.html>древе́сный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:питомник.html>пито́мник</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevésnyj</b> pitómnik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">arboretum; nursery forest</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wood pulp</li></ol>

***древко.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:древко.html>дре́вко</a> (18438)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древо.html>дре́во</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drévo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tree, wood</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ко</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ko</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">diminutive suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (stem-stressed variant) or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древо.html>дре́во</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drévo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ко́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (ending-stressed variant).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древко.html>дре́вко</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древко.html>древко́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drévko</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drevkó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древко.html>дре́вка</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древко.html>древка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древко.html>дре́вки</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древко.html>древки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древко.html>дре́вков</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древко.html>древко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>shaft, pole, staff
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древко.html>дре́вко</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знамя.html>зна́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:флаг.html>фла́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevko</b> známeni, flága</i> ― <span class="e-translation">flagstaff</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:древко.html>дре́вко</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пики.html>пи́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drevko</b> píki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pikestaff</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:древний.html>дре́вний</a> (1443)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*drevьňь</i>, an yo-stem variant of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*drevьnъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древний.html>дре́вний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drévnij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:древний.html>древне́е</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:древний.html>древне́й</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древнейший.html>древне́йший</a></b>)

<ol><li>ancient</li>
<li>antique, very old</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:древо.html>дре́во</a> (14886)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">дрѣво</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drěvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́рево</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dérevo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited Old East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древо.html>дре́во</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drévo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древо.html>дре́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древо.html>древеса́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:древо.html>древе́с</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic or literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tree</li></ol>

***дрейфить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрейфить.html>дре́йфить</a> (22749)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <a href = vnd.unilang:дрейф.html>дрейф</a>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрейфить.html>дре́йфить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dréjfitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сдре́йфить</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to quail, to funk, to show the white feather, to show cowardice</li></ol>

<p>From <a href = vnd.unilang:дрейф.html>дрейф</a>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрейфовать.html>дрейфова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drejfovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to drift <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to move slowly, pushed by currents of water, air, etc</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***дремать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дремать.html>дрема́ть</a> (3943)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*drěmati</i>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">дрѣмати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drěmati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to drowse, doze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">дремати</i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">dremati</i> and more distantly with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dormiō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I sleep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дремать.html>дрема́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dremátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подремать.html>подрема́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задремать.html>задрема́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздремнуть.html>вздремну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to doze, to slumber, to drowse
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2017</b>,  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">еле́на хае́цкая</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Jeléna Xajéckaja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,  <cite><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:космический.html>косми́ческая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тетушка.html>тётушка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Kosmíčeskaja tjótuška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взорваться.html>взорва́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шлюз.html>шлю́зы</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пьяный.html>пья́ный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> зю́зю, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:муза.html>му́зы</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:муза.html>му́зы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дремать.html>дре́млют</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дремать.html>дре́млют</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дремать.html>дре́млют</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>небеса́х</a>, — <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ла</a> бу́гго.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vzorválisʹ šljúzy, ty pʹjányj v zjúzju, i tólʹko múzy, tólʹko múzy ne <b>drémljut</b>, ne <b>drémljut</b>, ne <b>drémljut</b> v nebesáx, — skazála Búggo.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The gateways are blown up, you are drunk as judge, and only the muses, only the muses do not sleep, do not slumber, do not slumber, do not slumber in the heavens, said Buggo.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***дремота.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дремота.html>дремо́та</a> (14493)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дремать.html>дрема́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dremátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́та</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дремота.html>дремо́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dremóta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дремота.html>дремо́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дремота.html>дремо́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дремота.html>дремо́т</a></b>)
</p>
